through the archaeological evidence found throughout the game as well as in game lore so first of all let us justify why we are calling this period prehistory and what prehistory actually is prehistory in the real world is the period of human history that generally predates the invention of writing systems from the beginning of tool use and the development of societies up until the written word prehistory is generally marked by three major ages though there are various sub periods beneath these the Stone Age the Bronze Age and the iron age all named for the main material used for tools and weapons this is of course subject to variation Culture by culture region by region as human society Advanced and developed at different rates throughout the world but is a good General framework to begin to understand this period of History so with that in mind let us chart the evolution of beastman society through Elden Ring's prehistoric era as I have previously said personally
